<text>Shout out to Soukay the stylist who braided my hair. She specializes in African braiding, weaves, twists, and crocheting... the only thing she does not do is relaxers. I was a little apprehensive at first because she wasnt there when I arrived. However I do understand things can happen to make you a little  late. There was a caucasian lady waiting to get her hair weaved and I could tell she was a regular client which means the shop can style all races and all hair types. I was really surprised how gentle and how fast Soukay finished my hair.  When making an appointment be specific on which stylist you want to do your hair. <rating>4<//rating><UserId.>109148558281438214035</UserId.><name>3 Daoist</name>< Review>
We drank, we ate, we shivered.
Covid. Yeah it's winter and we sat out in the cold because we were excited to finally be able to enjoy a night out.
This was our second time at Inc 82 but the first was long ago and we don't remember it well.
We had some beers and we had some food. The beers were appreciated and expertly recommended by our server Aliyah. She also made some food recommendations which were appreciated but only taken in part by us. The wife loved the shrimp tacos and we kinda like the carne asada street tacos though they were a little dry. The cheese curds is where we strayed from her recommendations to our regret. They were overcooked and extremely dry. Once again proof that it's generally best to trust your server's recommendations.<//Review>

<Text>I only gave two stars because they have a fairly good size beer menu, but you cannot get more than one taster without paying a couple bucks for a taster. This is a ridiculous concept, especially if you have more than one brewery as an option for a particular type of brew. Makes no sense that you have to pay to taste both to decide what beer you want. Have never encountered this at any other tap house. Usually places have a limit to 4 tasters or so.
I will never go back because I can go to the other 20+ (exaggerating) places that allow free tasters. I'd understand if someone asks for a taster of Bud.

Nice setting, good bar games. Overall great place besides the dictatorship rules of beer tasting. Honestly, I think a majority of people go for the ambiance. If you really enjoy beer, and exploring flavors, then you're better off going somewhere else. If you want to feel cool and hip, and you go to places strictly for the ambiance, then this place is great.</Text>< resp>

Second time, and I just had to add a review. First experience was good (not great on account of a poor Moscow Mule), but the food - BBQ Chicken sandwich - was great.

On this visit I made the smart choice of ordering the Inc 82 burger and was blown away!

Pastrami plus sauerkraut and a fantastic beef patty; it's mouthwatering heaven. Curly garlic fries are a great addition to a great burger. I had a dark in-house ale that was equally good, stick to their beer, skip the cocktails.

But that burger, oh man that burger: unexpectedly good!

If you're looking for some high quality pub food in a cozy brewery atmosphere, then do yourself a favour and pay these guys a visit!</Review>

<pics>None< /pics><Response>None< /Response><Gmap_id>0x80c2b69fa0e8881d:0x7b20bbcbb71d9d8e<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>

None</response>
< Text>
Finally made it to this sports bar after driving by all the time on my way to the gym. I had no idea how it would look inside and to my surprise it was very nice! The decor is perfect. They have plenty of TVs all around for your sports enjoyment. It isn't very big, but it feels like you're at a sporting event. Loud, laughter, cheering, booing, etc., is all you here while you're there until the games are over and it gets quieter.
The day I went was very full, Dodger playoff game, UCLA Football and NFL were all on at the same time. We waited a little, but were seated in a waiting area and were allowed to order drinks while they found my friend and I a seat. It took about 10 minutes and we were sat in the mix of all the rukkus.
The selection of beers is great. Plenty to choose from whatever your liking may be. They did run out of one that I was interested in. Shows how popular it is. The food menu all looked delicious. I ended up ordering a chicken quesadilla, and my friend ordered chicken tacos. We both shared guacamole and chips. All of it was delicious!!!! The chicken was marinated perfectly. The presentation of the food was also really great.
Needless to say, I will be back at Flights to watch more sports and try out other items on their menu. Their wings and nachos looked so yummy but I was too stuffed to have more. Great service and plenty of parking!</Text>
